johnnydmad EX5 test console
Using ff6.smc as source
Playlist file is set to default.txt

press enter to continue or type:
    "chaos" to toggle chaotic mode
    "motif" to toggle motif mode (prefer songs from same game)
    "sfxv" to check songs for errors, sorted by longest sequence variant
    "mem" to check songs for errors, sorted by highest memory use variant
    "pool" to simulate many seeds and report the observed probability pools for each track
    "battle" to simulate many seeds and report probabilities for only battle music
    "pl FILENAME" to set FILENAME as playlist instead of default
    "dm FILENAME" to generate a test tierboss MML file including FILENAME
pool
